        });

    var cx = '005933198350176372664:riyhycsgqf4';

          <div class="node__content">

                  <div class="longform-layout longform-layout--content" style="padding: 25px; background-color: rgba(0,0,0,.50);">
                   <div class="envelope-hero__content__title">
                    Science of the Mind
                   </div>
                   <div class="envelope-hero__content__body">
                    <p>
                     A longstanding area of research excellence is now a popular new major
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     <a class="cta-button immersive-a" href="https://around.uoregon.edu/neuroscience?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=CTAbutton&amp;utm_campaign=immersive&amp;utm_content=CTAbutton">
                      Explore Neuroscience
                     </a>
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                <div class="longform-layout longform-layout--photos" data-uoes-title="Longform Text Content Width">

               </p>
               <div class="envelope-stories envelope-stories--no-green envelope-stories--no-flush">
                <div class="envelope-stories__story">
                 <div class="envelope-stories__photo">
                  <span class="align-center media media--type-image media--view-mode-crop-custom">

                 <div class="envelope-stories__content">
                  <div class="envelope-stories__title">
                   A year of uncertainty
                  </div>
                  <div class="envelope-stories__body">
                   <p>
                    From the earliest days of COVID-19, the UO community has stepped up to provide hope and answers during a global pandemic.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a class="cta-button immersive-b" href="https://around.uoregon.edu/covid-yearbook?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=CTAbutton&amp;utm_campaign=spotlight&amp;utm_content=CTAbutton">
                     COVID-19 Stories
                    </a>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="envelope-stories__story">
                 <div class="envelope-stories__photo">
                  <span class="align-center media media--type-image media--view-mode-crop-custom">
                   <span class="field field--name-field-media-image field--type-image field--label-hidden field__item">
                    <picture>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 1200px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_xl/public/2021-03/b-story-2021-things-in-eugene-1.jpg?itok=VculX2hs 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 960px) and (max-width: 1199px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_xl/public/2021-03/b-story-2021-things-in-eugene-1.jpg?itok=VculX2hs 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 660px) and (max-width: 959px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom/public/2021-03/b-story-2021-things-in-eugene-1.jpg?itok=ZXRe8Srk 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>

                <h2 style="text-align: center;">
                 Study Life in All Its Forms
                </h2>
                <p>
                 Want to study the life sciences—life and all living things—in the classroom, the lab, and natural habitats? We offer outstanding programs in
                 <a href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors/biochemistry?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major" style="color: #fee11a;">
                  <u>
                   biochemistry
                  </u>
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors/human-physiology?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major" style="color: #fee11a;">
                  <u>
                   human physiology
                  </u>
                 </a>
                 , and many facets of
                 <a href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors/biology?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major" style="color: #fee11a;">
                  <u>
                   biology
                  </u>
                 </a>
                 —including the only
                 <a href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors/marine-biology?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major" style="color: #fee11a;">
                  marine biology
                 </a>
                 program in the Pacific Northwest. Can't pick just one? Consider
                 <a href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors/general-science?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major" style="color: #fee11a;">
                  <u>
                   general science
                  </u>
                 </a>
                 , where you can choose a specialization tailored to your interests and career goals.
                </p>
                <p>
                 As a Tier 1 research institution, our renowned faculty provide practical training in state-of-the-art facilities to prepare you for a career in research, medicine, neuroscience, or other health-related disciplines.
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: center;">
                 <a class="cta-button cta-button--standard" href="https://admissions.uoregon.edu/majors?interest=190&amp;utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=CTAbutton&amp;utm_campaign=featured-major">
                  Dissect Biological Sciences Degrees
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>

                <div style="height: 10px;">
                </div>
                <h2 style="text-align: center;">
                 A Place for Curiosity
                </h2>
                <p>
                 Ducks dive into research to find answers to some of humanity’s biggest questions. We’re using big data to save and improve lives, striving to predict earthquakes and prevent deadly disease. We’re combining expertise across disciplines in math, biology, and genomics with bioengineering, neuroengineering, and precision medicine to fight cancer.
                </p>
                <p>
                 We’re re-defining research education with the
                 <strong>
                  <a href="https://accelerate.uoregon.edu/?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=research">
                   Phil and Penny Knight Campus for Accelerating Scientific Impact
                  </a>
                 </strong>
                 , shaping the next generation of scientists, innovators, and entrepreneurs, ready to serve the state, nation, and world with discovery and impact.
                </p>
                <p style="text-align: center;">
                 <a class="cta-button cta-button--submit" href="/research">
                  Oregon Research
                 </a>
                </p>
               </div>
               <div class="longform-layout longform-layout--wide">
                <div class="grid grid--strict grid--ato-4even grid--3col">

                    <span class="field__item">
                     <img alt="Icon of a Mortar Board" src="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/2021-02/mortar-board.svg" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <div style="height: 10px;">
                  </div>
                  <div class="big-number">
                   <div class="big-number__text">
                    90%
                   </div>
                   <div class="big-number__subtext">
                    of Knight Campus internship graduates are employed within 3 months
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="field__item">
             <div class="palette-bg-uo-green bg-pattern-molecules disable-link-icons envelope envelope--style-image envelope--standard envelope--style-black context--foreground-light">
              <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-envelope-content field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item">
               <div class="envelope-feature envelope-feature--text-right">
                <div class="envelope-feature__container">
                 <div class="envelope-feature__photo">
                  <span class="align-center media media--type-image media--view-mode-crop-custom">
                   <span class="field field--name-field-media-image field--type-image field--label-hidden field__item">
                    <picture>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 1200px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_xl/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=vO8mgNq4 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 960px) and (max-width: 1199px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_xl/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=vO8mgNq4 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 660px) and (max-width: 959px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=gsgmrKZv 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source media="all and (min-width: 320px) and (max-width: 659px)" srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_medium/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=y58iIg7h 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <source srcset="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_small/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=iNRJpMEI 1x" type="image/jpeg"/>
                     <img alt="Mars Rover" src="/sites/www1.uoregon.edu/files/styles/custom_small/public/2021-02/mars-rover.jpg?itok=iNRJpMEI" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
                    </picture>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="envelope-feature__content">
                  <div class="envelope-feature__content__title">
                   Friction from Mars Dust Poses Little Threat
                  </div>
                  <div class="envelope-feature__content__body">
                   <p>
                    Swirling Martian-like dust in a bottle in the lab of
                    <a href="https://pages.uoregon.edu/jdufek/">
                     Josef Dufek
                    </a>
                    , director of the
                    <a href="https://pages.uoregon.edu/volcanologycenter/">
                     Oregon Center for Volcanology
                    </a>
                    , indicates a low probability of large electrical storms or problems from static electricity from dust colliding with NASA’s exploration vehicles.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <a class="cta-button cta-button--standard" href="https://around.uoregon.edu/content/mars-rovers-safe-lightning-strikes-new-uo-research-finds?utm_source=homepage&amp;utm_medium=CTAbutton&amp;utm_campaign=research">
                     Strike Lightning
                    </a>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>

        <div class="settings-tray-editable block block-block-content block-block-contentcbe8e7b6-3222-49c6-9988-62bf79b75fce" data-drupal-settingstray="editable" id="block-utmcodepassthrough">
         <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item">
          <div>
           <script type="text/javascript">
            let queryString = window.location.search;

const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(queryString);
const utmParams = ['utm_source', 'utm_medium', 'utm_campaign', 'utm_term', 'utm_content'];
let pageLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.node__content a.utm-passthrough');

for (let pageLink of pageLinks) {
  let linkURL = encodeURI(pageLink.getAttribute('href'));
  let linkURLObject = new URL(linkURL, window.location);
  let originalURLObject = new URL(linkURL, window.location);
 
  for (let utmParam of utmParams) {
    let paramValue = urlParams.get(utmParam);

    if (paramValue != null) {
      linkURLObject.searchParams.set(utmParam, encodeURIComponent(paramValue));
    }
  }

  if (validURL(linkURLObject) && sameURL(originalURLObject, linkURLObject)) {
    pageLink.setAttribute('href',encodeURI(linkURLObject.toString()));
  }
}

function validURL(url) {
  let valid = true;

  if (!(url.protocol == 'http:' || url.protocol == 'https:')) {
    valid = false;
  }

  return valid;
}

function sameURL(luo, nuo) {
  if (luo.protocol != nuo.protocol) {
    return false;
  }
  if (luo.hostname != nuo.hostname) {
    return false;
  }
  if (luo.password != nuo.password) {
    return false;
  }
  if (luo.pathname != nuo.pathname) {
    return false;
  }
  if (luo.port != nuo.port) {
    return false;
  }
  if (luo.username != nuo.username) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}
           </script>
